# <a name="changelog-for-microsoft-graph"></a><span data-ttu-id="24109-101">Änderungsprotokoll für Microsoft Graph</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24109-101">Changelog for Microsoft Graph</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="24109-102">Dieses Änderungsprotokoll deckt alle Änderungen in Microsoft Graph ab, einschließlich der Version 1.0 und des Beta-Endpunkts von Microsoft Graph-APIs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24109-102">This changelog covers what's changed in Microsoft Graph, including the v1.0 and beta endpoint Microsoft Graph APIs.</span></span>

Use **sharepointIds** instead. </span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="24109-2179">Die **columnSet**-Eigenschaft von **listItem** zu **fields** umbenannt.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24109-2179">Renamed the **columnSet** property on **listItem** to **fields**.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="24109-2180">Geänderte **site**-Ressourcen, um den SharePoint-Hostnamen als Teil ihrer ID zu verwenden.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24109-2180">Changed **site** resources to use the SharePoint hostname as part of their ID.</span></span>
| <span data-ttu-id="24109-2181">Ergänzungen</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24109-2181">Addition</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="24109-2182">Beta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24109-2182">beta</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="24109-2183">Die **booleanColumn**-, **calculatedColumn**-, **choiceColumn**-, **dateTimeColumn**-, **lookupColumn**-, **numberColumn**-, **personOrGroupColumn**-, und **textColumn**-Ressourcentypen hinzugefügt.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24109-2183">Added the **booleanColumn**, **calculatedColumn**, **choiceColumn**, **dateTimeColumn**, **lookupColumn**, **numberColumn**, **personOrGroupColumn**, and **textColumn** resource types.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="24109-2184">Die **displayName**-Eigenschaft zu **site** hinzugefügt.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24109-2184">Added the **displayName** property to **site**.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="24109-2185">Die **columns**-Navigationseigenschaft zu **site** hinzugefügt.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24109-2185">Added the **columns** navigation property to **site**.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="24109-2186">**list**- und **listItem**- Navigationseigenschaften zu **sharedDriveItem** hinzugefügt.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24109-2186">Added the **list** and **listItem** navigation properties to **sharedDriveItem**.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="24109-2187">**sharepointIds**-Eigenschaft zu **list**, **listItem** und **site** hinzugefügt.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24109-2187">Added the **sharepointIds** property to **list** and **listItem**, and **site**.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="24109-2188">**columnDefinition**-Ressourcentyp hinzugefügt.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24109-2188">Added the **columnDefinition** resource type.</span></span>

## <a name="january-2017"></a><span data-ttu-id="24109-3004">Januar 2017</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24109-3004">January 2017</span></span>

### <a name="outlook-calendar"></a><span data-ttu-id="24109-3005">Outlook-Kalender</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24109-3005">Outlook calendar</span></span>

Dies bedeutet, dass Sie mithilfe dieser API keinen eingeladenen Benutzer mehr zu einer Gruppe hinzufügen können. This means that you will no longer be able to add an invited user to a group using this API. Instead, use the [add member API](https://developer.microsoft.com/de-DE/graph/docs/api-reference/v1.0/api/group_post_members) to add a user to a group.</span></span> |

These APIs allow for secure publishing of on-premises applications to users outside the corporate network using Azure AD as the common control plane for access. You can use the published APIs to write applications that can retrieve and update various aspects of application proxy, such as _connectors_, _connectorGroups_ and the _onPremisesPublishing_ settings of an application.</span></span> |

Any tokens issued before this time are invalid, and any attempt to use them would force a new sign-in for the user.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="24109-3374">Ergänzungen</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24109-3374">Addition</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="24109-3375">Beta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24109-3375">Beta</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="24109-3376">Die **showInAddressList**-Eigenschaft wurde hinzugefügt, mit der gesteuert wird, ob die globale Adressliste von Outlook diesen Benutzer enthalten soll.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24109-3376">Added **showInAddressList** property to control if the Outlook global address list should contain this user.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="24109-3377">Ergänzungen</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24109-3377">Addition</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="24109-3378">Beta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24109-3378">Beta</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="24109-3379">Die **invalidateAllRefreshTokens**-Dienstaktion wurde hinzugefügt, mit der alle Aktualisierungs- und Sitzungstoken des Benutzers, die für Anwendungen ausgestellt wurden, ungültig werden, indem die **refreshTokensValidFromDateTime**-Benutzereigenschaft auf aktuelles Datum und aktuelle Uhrzeit zurückgesetzt wird.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24109-3379">Added **invalidateAllRefreshTokens** service action that invalidates all of the user's refresh and session tokens issued to applications, by resetting the **refreshTokensValidFromDateTime** user property to the current date-time.</span></span> |

Beispiel: POST /drive/items/{item-id}/invite</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24109-p178">Added _invite_ function to send a sharing invitation to an existing item.
